To create a cross-exchange trading bot in Python that meets the customer's requirements, we will structure the application into multiple files. Below is a high-level overview of the core classes, functions, and methods that will be necessary for the implementation:

### Core Classes and Functions

1. **ConfigManager**
   - Purpose: Load and manage configuration settings from a settings file.

2. **ExchangeAPI**
   - Purpose: Abstract class to handle API interactions with exchanges (Poloniex and CoinEx).

3. **PoloniexAPI**
   - Purpose: Retrieve order-book and funding-rate data from Poloniex.

4. **CoinExAPI**
   - Purpose: Retrieve order-book and funding-rate data from CoinEx.

5. **TradingBot**
   - Purpose: Main bot logic to identify pricing gaps and execute trades.

6. **Analytics**
   - Purpose: Live analytics layer to recalculate spreads and fees.

7. **GUI**
   - Purpose: Graphical User Interface to interact with the bot.

### File Structure
1. `main.py` - Entry point of the application.
2. `config_manager.py` - Handles configuration settings.
3. `exchange_api.py` - Abstract class for exchange APIs.
4. `poloniex_api.py` - Implementation for Poloniex API.
5. `coinex_api.py` - Implementation for CoinEx API.
6. `trading_bot.py` - Contains the trading logic.
7. `analytics.py` - Contains the analytics logic.
8. `gui.py` - Contains the GUI implementation.

Now, let's implement each file.

### 1. `main.py`

```python
'''
Main entry point for the cross-exchange trading bot.
'''

from config_manager import ConfigManager
from trading_bot import TradingBot
from gui import GUI

def main():
    config = ConfigManager('config.json')
    trading_bot = TradingBot(config)
    gui = GUI(trading_bot)
    gui.run()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

### 2. `config_manager.py`

```python
'''
Handles loading and managing configuration settings from a JSON file.
'''

import json

class ConfigManager:
    def __init__(self, config_file):
        self.config_file = config_file
        self.settings = self.load_config()

    def load_config(self):
        with open(self.config_file, 'r') as file:
            return json.load(file)

    def get_setting(self, key):
        return self.settings.get(key)
```

### 3. `exchange_api.py`

```python
'''
Abstract class for handling API interactions with exchanges.
'''

class ExchangeAPI:
    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        raise NotImplementedError

    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        raise NotImplementedError
```

### 4. `poloniex_api.py`

```python
'''
Implementation for Poloniex API.
'''

import requests
from exchange_api import ExchangeAPI

class PoloniexAPI(ExchangeAPI):
    BASE_URL = 'https://api.poloniex.com'

    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/public?command=returnOrderBook&currencyPair={symbol}')
        return response.json()

    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/public?command=returnFundingInfo&currency={symbol}')
        return response.json()
```

### 5. `coinex_api.py`

```python
'''
Implementation for CoinEx API.
'''

import requests
from exchange_api import ExchangeAPI

class CoinExAPI(ExchangeAPI):
    BASE_URL = 'https://api.coinex.com/v1'

    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/market/depth?market={symbol}')
        return response.json()

    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/market/funding_rate?market={symbol}')
        return response.json()
```

### 6. `trading_bot.py`

```python
'''
Contains the trading logic for identifying pricing gaps and executing trades.
'''

from poloniex_api import PoloniexAPI
from coinex_api import CoinExAPI

class TradingBot:
    def __init__(self, config):
        self.config = config
        self.poloniex_api = PoloniexAPI()
        self.coinex_api = CoinExAPI()

    def identify_gaps(self, symbol):
        poloniex_order_book = self.poloniex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        coinex_order_book = self.coinex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        # Logic to identify pricing gaps
        # ...

    def execute_trade(self, symbol, amount):
        # Logic to execute trade
        # ...
        pass
```

### 7. `analytics.py`

```python
'''
Contains the analytics logic for recalculating spreads and fees.
'''

class Analytics:
    def __init__(self):
        pass

    def calculate_spread(self, bid_price, ask_price):
        return ask_price - bid_price

    def calculate_fees(self, amount, fee_rate):
        return amount * fee_rate
```

### 8. `gui.py`

```python
'''
Contains the GUI implementation for the trading bot.
'''

import tkinter as tk

class GUI:
    def __init__(self, trading_bot):
        self.trading_bot = trading_bot
        self.root = tk.Tk()
        self.root.title("Cross-Exchange Trading Bot")

    def run(self):
        self.create_widgets()
        self.root.mainloop()

    def create_widgets(self):
        # Create GUI components
        tk.Label(self.root, text="Trading Bot").pack()
        # Add more GUI elements as needed
```

This implementation provides a structured approach to building a cross-exchange trading bot in Python. Each file is responsible for a specific aspect of the application, ensuring modularity and ease of maintenance. The GUI allows users to interact with the bot visually, while the trading logic handles the core functionality of identifying pricing gaps and executing trades.

config_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles loading and managing configuration settings from a JSON file.
'''
import json
class ConfigManager:
    def __init__(self, config_file):
        self.config_file = config_file
        self.settings = self.load_config()
    def load_config(self):
        with open(self.config_file, 'r') as file:
            return json.load(file)
    def get_setting(self, key):
        return self.settings.get(key)
```

exchange_api.py
```python
'''
Abstract class for handling API interactions with exchanges.
'''
class ExchangeAPI:
    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        raise NotImplementedError
    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        raise NotImplementedError
```

poloniex_api.py
```python
'''
Implementation for Poloniex API.
'''
import requests
from exchange_api import ExchangeAPI
class PoloniexAPI(ExchangeAPI):
    BASE_URL = 'https://api.poloniex.com'
    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/public?command=returnOrderBook&currencyPair={symbol}')
        return response.json()
    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/public?command=returnFundingInfo&currency={symbol}')
        return response.json()
```

coinex_api.py
```python
'''
Implementation for CoinEx API.
'''
import requests
from exchange_api import ExchangeAPI
class CoinExAPI(ExchangeAPI):
    BASE_URL = 'https://api.coinex.com/v1'
    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/market/depth?market={symbol}')
        return response.json()
    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/market/funding_rate?market={symbol}')
        return response.json()
```

### trading_bot.py
```python
'''
Contains the trading logic for identifying pricing gaps and executing trades.
'''
from poloniex_api import PoloniexAPI
from coinex_api import CoinExAPI
from analytics import Analytics

class TradingBot:
    def __init__(self, config):
        self.config = config
        self.poloniex_api = PoloniexAPI()
        self.coinex_api = CoinExAPI()
        self.analytics = Analytics()
        self.position_size = self.config.get_setting('position_size')

    def identify_gaps(self, symbol):
        poloniex_order_book = self.poloniex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        coinex_order_book = self.coinex_api.get_order_book(symbol)

        # Extract bid and ask prices
        poloniex_bid = float(poloniex_order_book['bids'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book['bids'] else 0
        poloniex_ask = float(poloniex_order_book['asks'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book['asks'] else 0
        coinex_bid = float(coinex_order_book['data']['bids'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book['data']['bids'] else 0
        coinex_ask = float(coinex_order_book['data']['asks'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book['data']['asks'] else 0

        # Identify pricing gaps
        if poloniex_bid > coinex_ask:
            return 'buy', coinex_ask, self.position_size
        elif coinex_bid > poloniex_ask:
            return 'sell', poloniex_ask, self.position_size
        return None, None, None

    def execute_trade(self, symbol, amount, direction):
        # Logic to execute trade
        if direction == 'buy':
            print(f"Buying {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            # Add code to execute buy order
        elif direction == 'sell':
            print(f"Selling {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            # Add code to execute sell order

    def run(self, symbol):
        direction, price, amount = self.identify_gaps(symbol)
        if direction:
            self.execute_trade(symbol, amount, direction)
```

        self.settings = self.load_config()

### trading_bot.py
```python
'''
Contains the trading logic for identifying pricing gaps and executing trades.
'''
from poloniex_api import PoloniexAPI
from coinex_api import CoinExAPI
from analytics import Analytics

class TradingBot:
    def __init__(self, config):
        self.config = config
        self.poloniex_api = PoloniexAPI()
        self.coinex_api = CoinExAPI()
        self.analytics = Analytics()
        self.position_size = self.config.get_setting('position_size')

    def identify_gaps(self, symbol):
        poloniex_order_book = self.poloniex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        coinex_order_book = self.coinex_api.get_order_book(symbol)

        # Extract bid and ask prices
        poloniex_bid = float(poloniex_order_book['bids'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book['bids'] else 0
        poloniex_ask = float(poloniex_order_book['asks'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book['asks'] else 0
        coinex_bid = float(coinex_order_book['data']['bids'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book['data']['bids'] else 0
        coinex_ask = float(coinex_order_book['data']['asks'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book['data']['asks'] else 0

        # Identify pricing gaps
        if poloniex_bid > coinex_ask:
            return 'buy', coinex_ask, self.position_size
        elif coinex_bid > poloniex_ask:
            return 'sell', poloniex_ask, self.position_size
        return None, None, None

    def execute_trade(self, symbol, amount, direction):
        # Logic to execute trade
        if direction == 'buy':
            print(f"Buying {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            # Add code to execute buy order
        elif direction == 'sell':
            print(f"Selling {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            # Add code to execute sell order

    def run(self, symbol):
        direction, price, amount = self.identify_gaps(symbol)
        if direction:
            self.execute_trade(symbol, amount, direction)
```

    BASE_URL = 'https://api.coinex.com/v1'

    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/market/depth?market={symbol}')
        return response.json()

    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/market/funding_rate?market={symbol}')
        return response.json()
```

'''
Contains the analytics logic for recalculating spreads and fees.
'''
class Analytics:
    def __init__(self):
        pass

    def calculate_spread(self, bid_price, ask_price):
        return ask_price - bid_price

    def calculate_fees(self, amount, fee_rate):
        return amount * fee_rate

config_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles loading and managing configuration settings from a JSON file.
'''
import json
class ConfigManager:
    def __init__(self, config_file):
        self.config_file = config_file
        self.settings = self.load_config()
    def load_config(self):
        with open(self.config_file, 'r') as file:
            return json.load(file)
    def get_setting(self, key):
        return self.settings.get(key)
```

exchange_api.py
```python
'''
Abstract class for handling API interactions with exchanges.
'''
class ExchangeAPI:
    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        raise NotImplementedError
    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        raise NotImplementedError
```

poloniex_api.py
```python
'''
Implementation for Poloniex API.
'''
import requests
from exchange_api import ExchangeAPI
class PoloniexAPI(ExchangeAPI):
    BASE_URL = 'https://api.poloniex.com'
    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/public?command=returnOrderBook&currencyPair={symbol}')
        return response.json()
    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/public?command=returnFundingInfo&currency={symbol}')
        return response.json()
```

coinex_api.py
```python
'''
Implementation for CoinEx API.
'''
import requests
from exchange_api import ExchangeAPI
class CoinExAPI(ExchangeAPI):
    BASE_URL = 'https://api.coinex.com/v1'
    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/market/depth?market={symbol}')
        return response.json()
    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/market/funding_rate?market={symbol}')
        return response.json()
```

trading_bot.py
```python
'''
Contains the trading logic for identifying pricing gaps and executing trades.
'''
from poloniex_api import PoloniexAPI
from coinex_api import CoinExAPI
from analytics import Analytics
class TradingBot:
    def __init__(self, config):
        self.config = config
        self.poloniex_api = PoloniexAPI()
        self.coinex_api = CoinExAPI()
        self.analytics = Analytics()
        self.position_size = self.config.get_setting('position_size')
    def identify_gaps(self, symbol):
        poloniex_order_book = self.poloniex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        coinex_order_book = self.coinex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        # Extract bid and ask prices
        poloniex_bid = float(poloniex_order_book['bids'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book['bids'] else 0
        poloniex_ask = float(poloniex_order_book['asks'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book['asks'] else 0
        coinex_bid = float(coinex_order_book['data']['bids'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book['data']['bids'] else 0
        coinex_ask = float(coinex_order_book['data']['asks'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book['data']['asks'] else 0
        # Identify pricing gaps
        if poloniex_bid > coinex_ask:
            return 'buy', coinex_ask, self.position_size
        elif coinex_bid > poloniex_ask:
            return 'sell', poloniex_ask, self.position_size
        return None, None, None
    def execute_trade(self, symbol, amount, direction):
        # Logic to execute trade
        if direction == 'buy':
            print(f"Buying {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            # Add code to execute buy order
        elif direction == 'sell':
            print(f"Selling {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            # Add code to execute sell order
    def run(self, symbol):
        direction, price, amount = self.identify_gaps(symbol)
        if direction:
            self.execute_trade(symbol, amount, direction)
```

**analytics.py**
```python
'''
Contains the analytics logic for recalculating spreads and fees.
'''
class Analytics:
    def __init__(self):
        pass

    def calculate_spread(self, bid_price, ask_price):
        '''
        Calculates the spread between bid and ask prices.
        '''
        return ask_price - bid_price

    def calculate_fees(self, amount, fee_rate):
        '''
        Calculates the fees based on the amount and fee rate.
        '''
        return amount * fee_rate

    def recalculate_spreads_and_fees(self, bid_price, ask_price, fee_rate):
        '''
        Recalculates spreads and fees for given bid and ask prices.
        '''
        spread = self.calculate_spread(bid_price, ask_price)
        fees = self.calculate_fees(spread, fee_rate)
        return spread, fees
```

    config = ConfigManager('config.json')
    trading_bot = TradingBot(config)
    gui = GUI(trading_bot)

    main()

```python
'''
Handles loading and managing configuration settings from a JSON file.
'''
import json

class ConfigManager:
    def __init__(self, config_file):
        self.config_file = config_file
        self.settings = self.load_config()

    def load_config(self):
        with open(self.config_file, 'r') as file:
            return json.load(file)

    def get_setting(self, key):
        return self.settings.get(key)
```

**exchange_api.py**
```python
'''
Abstract class for handling API interactions with exchanges.
'''
class ExchangeAPI:
    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        raise NotImplementedError

    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        raise NotImplementedError
```

**poloniex_api.py**
```python
'''
Implementation for Poloniex API.
'''
import requests
from exchange_api import ExchangeAPI

class PoloniexAPI(ExchangeAPI):
    BASE_URL = 'https://api.poloniex.com'

    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/public?command=returnOrderBook&currencyPair={symbol}')
        return response.json()

    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/public?command=returnFundingInfo&currency={symbol}')
        return response.json()
```

**coinex_api.py**
```python
'''
Implementation for CoinEx API.
'''
import requests
from exchange_api import ExchangeAPI

class CoinExAPI(ExchangeAPI):
    BASE_URL = 'https://api.coinex.com/v1'

    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/market/depth?market={symbol}')
        return response.json()

    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/market/funding_rate?market={symbol}')
        return response.json()
```

**trading_bot.py**
```python
'''
Contains the trading logic for identifying pricing gaps and executing trades.
'''
from poloniex_api import PoloniexAPI
from coinex_api import CoinExAPI
from analytics import Analytics

class TradingBot:
    def __init__(self, config):
        self.config = config
        self.poloniex_api = PoloniexAPI()
        self.coinex_api = CoinExAPI()
        self.analytics = Analytics()
        self.position_size = self.config.get_setting('position_size')

    def identify_gaps(self, symbol):
        poloniex_order_book = self.poloniex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        coinex_order_book = self.coinex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        # Extract bid and ask prices
        poloniex_bid = float(poloniex_order_book['bids'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book['bids'] else 0
        poloniex_ask = float(poloniex_order_book['asks'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book['asks'] else 0
        coinex_bid = float(coinex_order_book['data']['bids'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book['data']['bids'] else 0
        coinex_ask = float(coinex_order_book['data']['asks'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book['data']['asks'] else 0
        # Identify pricing gaps
        if poloniex_bid > coinex_ask:
            return 'buy', coinex_ask, self.position_size
        elif coinex_bid > poloniex_ask:
            return 'sell', poloniex_ask, self.position_size
        return None, None, None

    def execute_trade(self, symbol, amount, direction):
        # Logic to execute trade
        if direction == 'buy':
            print(f"Buying {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            # Add code to execute buy order
        elif direction == 'sell':
            print(f"Selling {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            # Add code to execute sell order

    def run(self, symbol):
        direction, price, amount = self.identify_gaps(symbol)
        if direction:
            self.execute_trade(symbol, amount, direction)
```

**analytics.py**
```python
'''
Contains the analytics logic for recalculating spreads and fees.
'''
class Analytics:
    def __init__(self):
        pass

    def calculate_spread(self, bid_price, ask_price):
        '''
        Calculates the spread between bid and ask prices.
        '''
        return ask_price - bid_price

    def calculate_fees(self, amount, fee_rate):
        '''
        Calculates the fees based on the amount and fee rate.
        '''
        return amount * fee_rate

    def recalculate_spreads_and_fees(self, bid_price, ask_price, fee_rate):
        '''
        Recalculates spreads and fees for given bid and ask prices.
        '''
        spread = self.calculate_spread(bid_price, ask_price)
        fees = self.calculate_fees(spread, fee_rate)
        return spread, fees
```

**main.py**
```python
'''
Main entry point for the cross-exchange trading bot.
'''
from config_manager import ConfigManager
from trading_bot import TradingBot
from gui import GUI

def main():
    config = ConfigManager('config.json')
    trading_bot = TradingBot(config)
    gui = GUI(trading_bot)
    gui.run()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

        self.config_file = config_file
        self.settings = self.load_config()
    def load_config(self):
        with open(self.config_file, 'r') as file:
            return json.load(file)
    def get_setting(self, key):
        return self.settings.get(key)
```

import requests
from exchange_api import ExchangeAPI
class PoloniexAPI(ExchangeAPI):
    BASE_URL = 'https://api.poloniex.com'
    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/public?command=returnOrderBook&currencyPair={symbol}')
        return response.json()
    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/public?command=returnFundingInfo&currency={symbol}')
        return response.json()

trading_bot.py
```python
'''
Contains the trading logic for identifying pricing gaps and executing trades.
'''
from poloniex_api import PoloniexAPI
from coinex_api import CoinExAPI
from analytics import Analytics
class TradingBot:
    def __init__(self, config):
        self.config = config
        self.poloniex_api = PoloniexAPI()
        self.coinex_api = CoinExAPI()
        self.analytics = Analytics()
        self.position_size = self.config.get_setting('position_size')
    def identify_gaps(self, symbol):
        poloniex_order_book = self.poloniex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        coinex_order_book = self.coinex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        # Extract bid and ask prices
        poloniex_bid = float(poloniex_order_book['bids'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book['bids'] else 0
        poloniex_ask = float(poloniex_order_book['asks'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book['asks'] else 0
        coinex_bid = float(coinex_order_book['data']['bids'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book['data']['bids'] else 0
        coinex_ask = float(coinex_order_book['data']['asks'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book['data']['asks'] else 0
        # Identify pricing gaps
        if poloniex_bid > coinex_ask:
            return 'buy', coinex_ask, self.position_size
        elif coinex_bid > poloniex_ask:
            return 'sell', poloniex_ask, self.position_size
        return None, None, None
    def execute_trade(self, symbol, amount, direction):
        # Logic to execute trade
        if direction == 'buy':
            print(f"Buying {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            # Add code to execute buy order
        elif direction == 'sell':
            print(f"Selling {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            # Add code to execute sell order
    def run(self, symbol):
        direction, price, amount = self.identify_gaps(symbol)
        if direction:
            self.execute_trade(symbol, amount, direction)
```

analytics.py
```python
'''
Contains the analytics logic for recalculating spreads and fees.
'''
class Analytics:
    def __init__(self):
        pass
    def calculate_spread(self, bid_price, ask_price):
        '''
        Calculates the spread between bid and ask prices.
        '''
        return ask_price - bid_price
    def calculate_fees(self, amount, fee_rate):
        '''
        Calculates the fees based on the amount and fee rate.
        '''
        return amount * fee_rate
    def recalculate_spreads_and_fees(self, bid_price, ask_price, fee_rate):
        '''
        Recalculates spreads and fees for given bid and ask prices.
        '''
        spread = self.calculate_spread(bid_price, ask_price)
        fees = self.calculate_fees(spread, fee_rate)
        return spread, fees
```

'''
Contains the analytics logic for recalculating spreads and fees.
'''
class Analytics:
    def __init__(self):
        pass

    def calculate_spread(self, bid_price, ask_price):
        '''
        Calculates the spread between bid and ask prices.
        '''
        return ask_price - bid_price

    def calculate_fees(self, amount, fee_rate):
        '''
        Calculates the fees based on the amount and fee rate.
        '''
        return amount * fee_rate

    def recalculate_spreads_and_fees(self, bid_price, ask_price, fee_rate):
        '''
        Recalculates spreads and fees for given bid and ask prices.
        '''
        spread = self.calculate_spread(bid_price, ask_price)
        fees = self.calculate_fees(spread, fee_rate)
        return spread, fees

    def get_fee_rate(self, exchange):
        '''
        Retrieves the fee rate for the specified exchange.
        '''
        # Placeholder for actual fee rate retrieval logic
        if exchange == 'Poloniex':
            return 0.0025  # Example fee rate for Poloniex
        elif exchange == 'CoinEx':
            return 0.001  # Example fee rate for CoinEx
        return 0.0  # Default fee rate if not found

config_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles loading and managing configuration settings from a JSON file.
'''
import json
class ConfigManager:
    def __init__(self, config_file):
        self.config_file = config_file
        self.settings = self.load_config()
    def load_config(self):
        with open(self.config_file, 'r') as file:
            return json.load(file)
    def get_setting(self, key):
        return self.settings.get(key)
```

exchange_api.py
```python
'''
Abstract class for handling API interactions with exchanges.
'''
class ExchangeAPI:
    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        raise NotImplementedError
    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        raise NotImplementedError
```

poloniex_api.py
```python
'''
Implementation for Poloniex API.
'''
import requests
from exchange_api import ExchangeAPI
class PoloniexAPI(ExchangeAPI):
    BASE_URL = 'https://api.poloniex.com'
    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/public?command=returnOrderBook&currencyPair={symbol}')
        return response.json()
    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/public?command=returnFundingInfo&currency={symbol}')
        return response.json()
```

coinex_api.py
```python
'''
Implementation for CoinEx API.
'''
import requests
from exchange_api import ExchangeAPI
class CoinExAPI(ExchangeAPI):
    BASE_URL = 'https://api.coinex.com/v1'
    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/market/depth?market={symbol}')
        return response.json()
    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/market/funding_rate?market={symbol}')
        return response.json()
```

trading_bot.py
```python
'''
Contains the trading logic for identifying pricing gaps and executing trades.
'''
from poloniex_api import PoloniexAPI
from coinex_api import CoinExAPI
from analytics import Analytics
class TradingBot:
    def __init__(self, config):
        self.config = config
        self.poloniex_api = PoloniexAPI()
        self.coinex_api = CoinExAPI()
        self.analytics = Analytics()
        self.position_size = self.config.get_setting('position_size')
    def identify_gaps(self, symbol):
        poloniex_order_book = self.poloniex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        coinex_order_book = self.coinex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        # Extract bid and ask prices
        poloniex_bid = float(poloniex_order_book['bids'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book['bids'] else 0
        poloniex_ask = float(poloniex_order_book['asks'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book['asks'] else 0
        coinex_bid = float(coinex_order_book['data']['bids'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book['data']['bids'] else 0
        coinex_ask = float(coinex_order_book['data']['asks'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book['data']['asks'] else 0
        # Identify pricing gaps
        if poloniex_bid > coinex_ask:
            return 'buy', coinex_ask, self.position_size
        elif coinex_bid > poloniex_ask:
            return 'sell', poloniex_ask, self.position_size
        return None, None, None
    def execute_trade(self, symbol, amount, direction):
        # Logic to execute trade
        if direction == 'buy':
            print(f"Buying {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            # Add code to execute buy order
        elif direction == 'sell':
            print(f"Selling {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            # Add code to execute sell order
    def run(self, symbol):
        direction, price, amount = self.identify_gaps(symbol)
        if direction:
            self.execute_trade(symbol, amount, direction)
```

analytics.py
```python
'''
Contains the analytics logic for recalculating spreads and fees.
'''
class Analytics:
    def __init__(self):
        pass
    def calculate_spread(self, bid_price, ask_price):
        '''
        Calculates the spread between bid and ask prices.
        '''
        return ask_price - bid_price
    def calculate_fees(self, amount, fee_rate):
        '''
        Calculates the fees based on the amount and fee rate.
        '''
        return amount * fee_rate
    def recalculate_spreads_and_fees(self, bid_price, ask_price, fee_rate):
        '''
        Recalculates spreads and fees for given bid and ask prices.
        '''
        spread = self.calculate_spread(bid_price, ask_price)
        fees = self.calculate_fees(spread, fee_rate)
        return spread, fees
    def get_fee_rate(self, exchange):
        '''
        Retrieves the fee rate for the specified exchange.
        '''
        # Placeholder for actual fee rate retrieval logic
        if exchange == 'Poloniex':
            return 0.0025  # Example fee rate for Poloniex
        elif exchange == 'CoinEx':
            return 0.001  # Example fee rate for CoinEx
        return 0.0  # Default fee rate if not found
```

### trading_bot.py
```python
'''
Contains the trading logic for identifying pricing gaps and executing trades.
'''
from poloniex_api import PoloniexAPI
from coinex_api import CoinExAPI
from analytics import Analytics

class TradingBot:
    def __init__(self, config):
        self.config = config
        self.poloniex_api = PoloniexAPI()
        self.coinex_api = CoinExAPI()
        self.analytics = Analytics()
        self.position_size = self.config.get_setting('position_size')

    def identify_gaps(self, symbol):
        poloniex_order_book = self.poloniex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        coinex_order_book = self.coinex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        # Extract bid and ask prices
        poloniex_bid = float(poloniex_order_book['bids'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book['bids'] else 0
        poloniex_ask = float(poloniex_order_book['asks'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book['asks'] else 0
        coinex_bid = float(coinex_order_book['data']['bids'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book['data']['bids'] else 0
        coinex_ask = float(coinex_order_book['data']['asks'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book['data']['asks'] else 0
        # Identify pricing gaps
        if poloniex_bid > coinex_ask:
            return 'buy', coinex_ask, self.position_size
        elif coinex_bid > poloniex_ask:
            return 'sell', poloniex_ask, self.position_size
        return None, None, None

    def execute_trade(self, symbol, amount, direction):
        # Logic to execute trade
        if direction == 'buy':
            print(f"Buying {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            # Add code to execute buy order
        elif direction == 'sell':
            print(f"Selling {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            # Add code to execute sell order

    def run(self, symbol):
        direction, price, amount = self.identify_gaps(symbol)
        if direction:
            self.execute_trade(symbol, amount, direction)
```

### analytics.py
```python
'''
Contains the analytics logic for recalculating spreads and fees.
'''
class Analytics:
    def __init__(self):
        pass

    def calculate_spread(self, bid_price, ask_price):
        '''
        Calculates the spread between bid and ask prices.
        '''
        return ask_price - bid_price

    def calculate_fees(self, amount, fee_rate):
        '''
        Calculates the fees based on the amount and fee rate.
        '''
        return amount * fee_rate

    def recalculate_spreads_and_fees(self, bid_price, ask_price, fee_rate):
        '''
        Recalculates spreads and fees for given bid and ask prices.
        '''
        spread = self.calculate_spread(bid_price, ask_price)
        fees = self.calculate_fees(spread, fee_rate)
        return spread, fees

    def get_fee_rate(self, exchange):
        '''
        Retrieves the fee rate for the specified exchange.
        '''
        # Placeholder for actual fee rate retrieval logic
        if exchange == 'Poloniex':
            return 0.0025  # Example fee rate for Poloniex
        elif exchange == 'CoinEx':
            return 0.001  # Example fee rate for CoinEx
        return 0.0  # Default fee rate if not found
```

### poloniex_api.py
```python
'''
Implementation for Poloniex API.
'''
import requests
from exchange_api import ExchangeAPI

class PoloniexAPI(ExchangeAPI):
    BASE_URL = 'https://api.poloniex.com'

    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/public?command=returnOrderBook&currencyPair={symbol}')
        return response.json()

    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/public?command=returnFundingInfo&currency={symbol}')
        return response.json()
```

### coinex_api.py

'''
Implementation for CoinEx API.
'''
import requests
from exchange_api import ExchangeAPI

class CoinExAPI(ExchangeAPI):
    BASE_URL = 'https://api.coinex.com/v1'

    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/market/depth?market={symbol}')
        return response.json()

    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/market/funding_rate?market={symbol}')
        return response.json()
```

### trading_bot.py
```python
'''
Contains the trading logic for identifying pricing gaps and executing trades.
'''
from poloniex_api import PoloniexAPI
from coinex_api import CoinExAPI
from analytics import Analytics

class TradingBot:
    def __init__(self, config):
        self.config = config
        self.poloniex_api = PoloniexAPI()
        self.coinex_api = CoinExAPI()
        self.analytics = Analytics()
        self.position_size = self.config.get_setting('position_size')

    def identify_gaps(self, symbol):
        poloniex_order_book = self.poloniex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        coinex_order_book = self.coinex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        # Extract bid and ask prices
        poloniex_bid = float(poloniex_order_book['bids'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book['bids'] else 0
        poloniex_ask = float(poloniex_order_book['asks'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book['asks'] else 0
        coinex_bid = float(coinex_order_book['data']['bids'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book['data']['bids'] else 0
        coinex_ask = float(coinex_order_book['data']['asks'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book['data']['asks'] else 0
        # Identify pricing gaps
        if poloniex_bid > coinex_ask:
            return 'buy', coinex_ask, self.position_size
        elif coinex_bid > poloniex_ask:
            return 'sell', poloniex_ask, self.position_size
        return None, None, None

    def execute_trade(self, symbol, amount, direction):
        # Logic to execute trade
        if direction == 'buy':
            print(f"Buying {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            # Add code to execute buy order
        elif direction == 'sell':
            print(f"Selling {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            # Add code to execute sell order

    def run(self, symbol):
        direction, price, amount = self.identify_gaps(symbol)
        if direction:
            self.execute_trade(symbol, amount, direction)
```

### analytics.py
```python
'''
Contains the analytics logic for recalculating spreads and fees.
'''
class Analytics:
    def __init__(self):
        pass

    def calculate_spread(self, bid_price, ask_price):
        '''
        Calculates the spread between bid and ask prices.
        '''
        return ask_price - bid_price

    def calculate_fees(self, amount, fee_rate):
        '''
        Calculates the fees based on the amount and fee rate.
        '''
        return amount * fee_rate

    def recalculate_spreads_and_fees(self, bid_price, ask_price, fee_rate):
        '''
        Recalculates spreads and fees for given bid and ask prices.
        '''
        spread = self.calculate_spread(bid_price, ask_price)
        fees = self.calculate_fees(spread, fee_rate)
        return spread, fees

    def get_fee_rate(self, exchange):
        '''
        Retrieves the fee rate for the specified exchange.
        '''
        # Placeholder for actual fee rate retrieval logic
        if exchange == 'Poloniex':
            return 0.0025  # Example fee rate for Poloniex
        elif exchange == 'CoinEx':
            return 0.001  # Example fee rate for CoinEx
        return 0.0  # Default fee rate if not found
```

        self.root.title("Cross-Exchange Trading Bot")

    def run(self):
        self.create_widgets()
        self.root.mainloop()

    def create_widgets(self):
        # Create GUI components
        tk.Label(self.root, text="Trading Bot").pack()
        # Add more GUI elements as needed

config_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles loading and managing configuration settings from a JSON file.
'''
import json
class ConfigManager:
    def __init__(self, config_file):
        self.config_file = config_file
        self.settings = self.load_config()
    def load_config(self):
        with open(self.config_file, 'r') as file:
            return json.load(file)
    def get_setting(self, key):
        return self.settings.get(key)
```

'''
Abstract class for handling API interactions with exchanges.
'''
class ExchangeAPI:
    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        raise NotImplementedError
    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        raise NotImplementedError

'''
Implementation for Poloniex API.

import requests
from exchange_api import ExchangeAPI
class PoloniexAPI(ExchangeAPI):
    BASE_URL = 'https://api.poloniex.com'
    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/public?command=returnOrderBook&currencyPair={symbol}')
        return response.json()
    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/public?command=returnFundingInfo&currency={symbol}')
        return response.json()

'''

from poloniex_api import PoloniexAPI
from coinex_api import CoinExAPI
from analytics import Analytics
class TradingBot:
    def __init__(self, config):
        self.config = config
        self.poloniex_api = PoloniexAPI()
        self.coinex_api = CoinExAPI()
        self.analytics = Analytics()
        self.position_size = self.config.get_setting('position_size')
    def identify_gaps(self, symbol):
        poloniex_order_book = self.poloniex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        coinex_order_book = self.coinex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        # Extract bid and ask prices
        poloniex_bid = float(poloniex_order_book['bids'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book['bids'] else 0
        poloniex_ask = float(poloniex_order_book['asks'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book['asks'] else 0
        coinex_bid = float(coinex_order_book['data']['bids'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book['data']['bids'] else 0
        coinex_ask = float(coinex_order_book['data']['asks'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book['data']['asks'] else 0
        # Identify pricing gaps
        if poloniex_bid > coinex_ask:
            return 'buy', coinex_ask, self.position_size
        elif coinex_bid > poloniex_ask:
            return 'sell', poloniex_ask, self.position_size
        return None, None, None
    def execute_trade(self, symbol, amount, direction):
        # Logic to execute trade
        if direction == 'buy':
            print(f"Buying {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            # Add code to execute buy order
        elif direction == 'sell':
            print(f"Selling {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            # Add code to execute sell order
    def run(self, symbol):
        direction, price, amount = self.identify_gaps(symbol)
        if direction:
            self.execute_trade(symbol, amount, direction)

        Calculates the fees based on the amount and fee rate.

        return amount * fee_rate
    def recalculate_spreads_and_fees(self, bid_price, ask_price, fee_rate):
        '''
        Recalculates spreads and fees for given bid and ask prices.

        spread = self.calculate_spread(bid_price, ask_price)
        fees = self.calculate_fees(spread, fee_rate)
        return spread, fees

'''
Main entry point for the cross-exchange trading bot.
'''
from config_manager import ConfigManager
from trading_bot import TradingBot
from gui import GUI
def main():
    config = ConfigManager('config.json')
    trading_bot = TradingBot(config)
    gui = GUI(trading_bot)
    gui.run()

    main()

config_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles loading and managing configuration settings from a JSON file.
'''
import json
class ConfigManager:
    def __init__(self, config_file):
        self.config_file = config_file
        self.settings = self.load_config()
    def load_config(self):
        with open(self.config_file, 'r') as file:
            return json.load(file)
    def get_setting(self, key):
        return self.settings.get(key)
```

exchange_api.py
```python
'''
Abstract class for handling API interactions with exchanges.
'''
class ExchangeAPI:
    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        raise NotImplementedError
    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        raise NotImplementedError
```

poloniex_api.py
```python
'''
Implementation for Poloniex API.
'''
import requests
from exchange_api import ExchangeAPI
class PoloniexAPI(ExchangeAPI):
    BASE_URL = 'https://api.poloniex.com'
    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/public?command=returnOrderBook&currencyPair={symbol}')
        return response.json()
    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/public?command=returnFundingInfo&currency={symbol}')
        return response.json()
```

coinex_api.py
```python
'''
Implementation for CoinEx API.
'''
import requests
from exchange_api import ExchangeAPI
class CoinExAPI(ExchangeAPI):
    BASE_URL = 'https://api.coinex.com/v1'
    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/market/depth?market={symbol}')
        return response.json()
    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/market/funding_rate?market={symbol}')
        return response.json()
```

trading_bot.py
```python
'''
Contains the trading logic for identifying pricing gaps and executing trades.
'''
from poloniex_api import PoloniexAPI
from coinex_api import CoinExAPI
from analytics import Analytics
class TradingBot:
    def __init__(self, config):
        self.config = config
        self.poloniex_api = PoloniexAPI()
        self.coinex_api = CoinExAPI()
        self.analytics = Analytics()
        self.position_size = self.config.get_setting('position_size')
    def identify_gaps(self, symbol):
        poloniex_order_book = self.poloniex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        coinex_order_book = self.coinex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        # Extract bid and ask prices
        poloniex_bid = float(poloniex_order_book['bids'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book['bids'] else 0
        poloniex_ask = float(poloniex_order_book['asks'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book['asks'] else 0
        coinex_bid = float(coinex_order_book['data']['bids'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book['data']['bids'] else 0
        coinex_ask = float(coinex_order_book['data']['asks'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book['data']['asks'] else 0
        # Identify pricing gaps
        if poloniex_bid > coinex_ask:
            return 'buy', coinex_ask, self.position_size
        elif coinex_bid > poloniex_ask:
            return 'sell', poloniex_ask, self.position_size
        return None, None, None
    def execute_trade(self, symbol, amount, direction):
        # Logic to execute trade
        if direction == 'buy':
            print(f"Buying {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            # Add code to execute buy order
        elif direction == 'sell':
            print(f"Selling {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            # Add code to execute sell order
    def run(self, symbol):
        direction, price, amount = self.identify_gaps(symbol)
        if direction:
            self.execute_trade(symbol, amount, direction)
```

analytics.py
```python
'''
Contains the analytics logic for recalculating spreads and fees.
'''
class Analytics:
    def __init__(self):
        pass
    def calculate_spread(self, bid_price, ask_price):
        '''
        Calculates the spread between bid and ask prices.
        '''
        return ask_price - bid_price
    def calculate_fees(self, amount, fee_rate):
        '''
        Calculates the fees based on the amount and fee rate.
        '''
        return amount * fee_rate
    def recalculate_spreads_and_fees(self, bid_price, ask_price, fee_rate):
        '''
        Recalculates spreads and fees for given bid and ask prices.
        '''
        spread = self.calculate_spread(bid_price, ask_price)
        fees = self.calculate_fees(spread, fee_rate)
        return spread, fees
    def get_fee_rate(self, exchange):
        '''
        Retrieves the fee rate for the specified exchange.
        '''
        # Placeholder for actual fee rate retrieval logic
        if exchange == 'Poloniex':
            return 0.0025  # Example fee rate for Poloniex
        elif exchange == 'CoinEx':
            return 0.001  # Example fee rate for CoinEx
        return 0.0  # Default fee rate if not found

config_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles loading and managing configuration settings from a JSON file.
'''
import json

class ConfigManager:
    def __init__(self, config_file):
        self.config_file = config_file
        self.settings = self.load_config()

    def load_config(self):
        with open(self.config_file, 'r') as file:
            return json.load(file)

    def get_setting(self, key):
        return self.settings.get(key)
```

poloniex_api.py
```python
'''
Implementation for Poloniex API.
'''
import requests
from exchange_api import ExchangeAPI

class PoloniexAPI(ExchangeAPI):
    BASE_URL = 'https://api.poloniex.com'

    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        try:
            response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/public?command=returnOrderBook&currencyPair={symbol}')
            response.raise_for_status()  # Raises an error for bad responses
            return response.json()
        except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
            print(f"Error fetching order book: {e}")
            return {}

    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        try:
            response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/public?command=returnFundingInfo&currency={symbol}')
            response.raise_for_status()
            return response.json()
        except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
            print(f"Error fetching funding rate: {e}")
            return {}

    def place_order(self, symbol, amount, direction):
        # Placeholder for actual order placement logic
        print(f"Placing {direction} order for {amount} of {symbol} on Poloniex.")
```

coinex_api.py
```python
'''
Implementation for CoinEx API.
'''
import requests
from exchange_api import ExchangeAPI

class CoinExAPI(ExchangeAPI):
    BASE_URL = 'https://api.coinex.com/v1'

    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        try:
            response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/market/depth?market={symbol}')
            response.raise_for_status()
            return response.json()
        except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
            print(f"Error fetching order book: {e}")
            return {}

    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        try:
            response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/market/funding_rate?market={symbol}')
            response.raise_for_status()
            return response.json()
        except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
            print(f"Error fetching funding rate: {e}")
            return {}

    def place_order(self, symbol, amount, direction):
        # Placeholder for actual order placement logic
        print(f"Placing {direction} order for {amount} of {symbol} on CoinEx.")
```

trading_bot.py
```python
'''
Contains the trading logic for identifying pricing gaps and executing trades.
'''
from poloniex_api import PoloniexAPI
from coinex_api import CoinExAPI
from analytics import Analytics

class TradingBot:
    def __init__(self, config):
        self.config = config
        self.poloniex_api = PoloniexAPI()
        self.coinex_api = CoinExAPI()
        self.analytics = Analytics()
        self.position_size = self.config.get_setting('position_size')

    def identify_gaps(self, symbol):
        poloniex_order_book = self.poloniex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        coinex_order_book = self.coinex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        # Extract bid and ask prices
        poloniex_bid = float(poloniex_order_book['bids'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book['bids'] else 0
        poloniex_ask = float(poloniex_order_book['asks'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book['asks'] else 0
        coinex_bid = float(coinex_order_book['data']['bids'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book['data']['bids'] else 0
        coinex_ask = float(coinex_order_book['data']['asks'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book['data']['asks'] else 0
        # Identify pricing gaps
        if poloniex_bid > coinex_ask:
            return 'buy', coinex_ask, self.position_size
        elif coinex_bid > poloniex_ask:
            return 'sell', poloniex_ask, self.position_size
        return None, None, None

    def execute_trade(self, symbol, amount, direction):
        # Logic to execute trade
        if direction == 'buy':
            print(f"Buying {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            self.poloniex_api.place_order(symbol, amount, 'buy')
        elif direction == 'sell':
            print(f"Selling {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            self.coinex_api.place_order(symbol, amount, 'sell')

    def run(self, symbol):
        direction, price, amount = self.identify_gaps(symbol)
        if direction:
            self.execute_trade(symbol, amount, direction)
```

'''

class Analytics:
    def __init__(self):
        pass

    def calculate_spread(self, bid_price, ask_price):
        '''
        Calculates the spread between bid and ask prices.
        '''
        return ask_price - bid_price

    def calculate_fees(self, amount, fee_rate):
        '''
        Calculates the fees based on the amount and fee rate.
        '''
        return amount * fee_rate

    def recalculate_spreads_and_fees(self, bid_price, ask_price, fee_rate):
        '''
        Recalculates spreads and fees for given bid and ask prices.
        '''
        spread = self.calculate_spread(bid_price, ask_price)
        fees = self.calculate_fees(spread, fee_rate)
        return spread, fees

    def get_fee_rate(self, exchange):
        '''
        Retrieves the fee rate for the specified exchange.
        '''
        # Placeholder for actual fee rate retrieval logic
        if exchange == 'Poloniex':
            return 0.0025  # Example fee rate for Poloniex
        elif exchange == 'CoinEx':
            return 0.001  # Example fee rate for CoinEx
        return 0.0  # Default fee rate if not found

trading_bot.py
```python
'''
Contains the trading logic for identifying pricing gaps and executing trades.
'''
from poloniex_api import PoloniexAPI
from coinex_api import CoinExAPI
from analytics import Analytics

class TradingBot:
    def __init__(self, config):
        self.config = config
        self.poloniex_api = PoloniexAPI()
        self.coinex_api = CoinExAPI()
        self.analytics = Analytics()
        self.position_size = self.config.get_setting('position_size')

    def identify_gaps(self, symbol):
        poloniex_order_book = self.poloniex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        coinex_order_book = self.coinex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        # Extract bid and ask prices
        poloniex_bid = float(poloniex_order_book['bids'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book['bids'] else 0
        poloniex_ask = float(poloniex_order_book['asks'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book['asks'] else 0
        coinex_bid = float(coinex_order_book['data']['bids'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book['data']['bids'] else 0
        coinex_ask = float(coinex_order_book['data']['asks'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book['data']['asks'] else 0
        # Identify pricing gaps
        if poloniex_bid > coinex_ask:
            return 'buy', coinex_ask, self.position_size
        elif coinex_bid > poloniex_ask:
            return 'sell', poloniex_ask, self.position_size
        return None, None, None

    def execute_trade(self, symbol, amount, direction):
        # Logic to execute trade
        if direction == 'buy':
            print(f"Buying {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            self.poloniex_api.place_order(symbol, amount, 'buy')
        elif direction == 'sell':
            print(f"Selling {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            self.coinex_api.place_order(symbol, amount, 'sell')

    def run(self, symbol):
        direction, price, amount = self.identify_gaps(symbol)
        if direction:
            self.execute_trade(symbol, amount, direction)
```

'''
Main entry point for the cross-exchange trading bot.
'''
from config_manager import ConfigManager
from trading_bot import TradingBot
from gui import GUI
def main():
    config = ConfigManager('config.json')
    trading_bot = TradingBot(config)
    gui = GUI(trading_bot)
    gui.run()

config_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles loading and managing configuration settings from a JSON file.
'''
import json
class ConfigManager:
    def __init__(self, config_file):
        self.config_file = config_file
        self.settings = self.load_config()
    def load_config(self):
        with open(self.config_file, 'r') as file:
            return json.load(file)
    def get_setting(self, key):
        return self.settings.get(key)
```

exchange_api.py
```python
'''
Abstract class for handling API interactions with exchanges.
'''
class ExchangeAPI:
    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        raise NotImplementedError
    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        raise NotImplementedError
    def place_order(self, symbol, amount, direction):
        raise NotImplementedError
```

poloniex_api.py
```python
'''
Implementation for Poloniex API.
'''
import requests
from exchange_api import ExchangeAPI
class PoloniexAPI(ExchangeAPI):
    BASE_URL = 'https://api.poloniex.com'
    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        try:
            response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/public?command=returnOrderBook&currencyPair={symbol}')
            response.raise_for_status()  # Raises an error for bad responses
            return response.json()
        except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
            print(f"Error fetching order book: {e}")
            return {}
    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        try:
            response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/public?command=returnFundingInfo&currency={symbol}')
            response.raise_for_status()
            return response.json()
        except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
            print(f"Error fetching funding rate: {e}")
            return {}
    def place_order(self, symbol, amount, direction):
        # Placeholder for actual order placement logic
        print(f"Placing {direction} order for {amount} of {symbol} on Poloniex.")
```

coinex_api.py
```python
'''
Implementation for CoinEx API.
'''
import requests
from exchange_api import ExchangeAPI
class CoinExAPI(ExchangeAPI):
    BASE_URL = 'https://api.coinex.com/v1'
    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        try:
            response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/market/depth?market={symbol}')
            response.raise_for_status()
            return response.json()
        except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
            print(f"Error fetching order book: {e}")
            return {}
    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        try:
            response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/market/funding_rate?market={symbol}')
            response.raise_for_status()
            return response.json()
        except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
            print(f"Error fetching funding rate: {e}")
            return {}
    def place_order(self, symbol, amount, direction):
        # Placeholder for actual order placement logic
        print(f"Placing {direction} order for {amount} of {symbol} on CoinEx.")
```

trading_bot.py
```python
'''
Contains the trading logic for identifying pricing gaps and executing trades.
'''
from poloniex_api import PoloniexAPI
from coinex_api import CoinExAPI
from analytics import Analytics
class TradingBot:
    def __init__(self, config):
        self.config = config
        self.poloniex_api = PoloniexAPI()
        self.coinex_api = CoinExAPI()
        self.analytics = Analytics()
        self.position_size = self.config.get_setting('position_size')
    def identify_gaps(self, symbol):
        poloniex_order_book = self.poloniex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        coinex_order_book = self.coinex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        # Extract bid and ask prices
        poloniex_bid = float(poloniex_order_book['bids'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book['bids'] else 0
        poloniex_ask = float(poloniex_order_book['asks'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book['asks'] else 0
        coinex_bid = float(coinex_order_book['data']['bids'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book['data']['bids'] else 0
        coinex_ask = float(coinex_order_book['data']['asks'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book['data']['asks'] else 0
        # Identify pricing gaps
        if poloniex_bid > coinex_ask:
            return 'buy', coinex_ask, self.position_size
        elif coinex_bid > poloniex_ask:
            return 'sell', poloniex_ask, self.position_size
        return None, None, None
    def execute_trade(self, symbol, amount, direction):
        # Logic to execute trade
        if direction == 'buy':
            print(f"Buying {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            self.poloniex_api.place_order(symbol, amount, 'buy')
        elif direction == 'sell':
            print(f"Selling {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            self.coinex_api.place_order(symbol, amount, 'sell')
    def run(self, symbol):
        direction, price, amount = self.identify_gaps(symbol)
        if direction:
            self.execute_trade(symbol, amount, direction)
```

analytics.py
```python
'''
Contains the analytics logic for recalculating spreads and fees.
'''
class Analytics:
    def __init__(self):
        pass
    def calculate_spread(self, bid_price, ask_price):
        '''
        Calculates the spread between bid and ask prices.
        '''
        return ask_price - bid_price
    def calculate_fees(self, amount, fee_rate):
        '''
        Calculates the fees based on the amount and fee rate.
        '''
        return amount * fee_rate
    def recalculate_spreads_and_fees(self, bid_price, ask_price, fee_rate):
        '''
        Recalculates spreads and fees for given bid and ask prices.
        '''
        spread = self.calculate_spread(bid_price, ask_price)
        fees = self.calculate_fees(spread, fee_rate)
        return spread, fees
    def get_fee_rate(self, exchange):
        '''
        Retrieves the fee rate for the specified exchange.
        '''
        # Placeholder for actual fee rate retrieval logic
        if exchange == 'Poloniex':
            return 0.0025  # Example fee rate for Poloniex
        elif exchange == 'CoinEx':
            return 0.001  # Example fee rate for CoinEx
        return 0.0  # Default fee rate if not found
```

        self.root.title("Cross-Exchange Trading Bot")
    def run(self):
        self.create_widgets()
        self.root.mainloop()
    def create_widgets(self):
        # Create GUI components
        tk.Label(self.root, text="Trading Bot").pack()
        # Add more GUI elements as needed

config_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles loading and managing configuration settings from a JSON file.
'''
import json
class ConfigManager:
    def __init__(self, config_file):
        self.config_file = config_file
        self.settings = self.load_config()
    def load_config(self):
        with open(self.config_file, 'r') as file:
            return json.load(file)
    def get_setting(self, key):
        return self.settings.get(key)
```

poloniex_api.py
```python
'''
Implementation for Poloniex API.
'''
import requests
from exchange_api import ExchangeAPI
class PoloniexAPI(ExchangeAPI):
    BASE_URL = 'https://api.poloniex.com'
    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        try:
            response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/public?command=returnOrderBook&currencyPair={symbol}')
            response.raise_for_status()  # Raises an error for bad responses
            return response.json()
        except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
            print(f"Error fetching order book: {e}")
            return {}
    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        try:
            response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/public?command=returnFundingInfo&currency={symbol}')
            response.raise_for_status()
            return response.json()
        except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
            print(f"Error fetching funding rate: {e}")
            return {}
    def place_order(self, symbol, amount, direction):
        # Placeholder for actual order placement logic
        print(f"Placing {direction} order for {amount} of {symbol} on Poloniex.")
```

coinex_api.py
```python
'''
Implementation for CoinEx API.
'''
import requests
from exchange_api import ExchangeAPI
class CoinExAPI(ExchangeAPI):
    BASE_URL = 'https://api.coinex.com/v1'
    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        try:
            response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/market/depth?market={symbol}')
            response.raise_for_status()
            return response.json()
        except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
            print(f"Error fetching order book: {e}")
            return {}
    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        try:
            response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/market/funding_rate?market={symbol}')
            response.raise_for_status()
            return response.json()
        except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
            print(f"Error fetching funding rate: {e}")
            return {}
    def place_order(self, symbol, amount, direction):
        # Placeholder for actual order placement logic
        print(f"Placing {direction} order for {amount} of {symbol} on CoinEx.")
```

trading_bot.py
```python
'''
Contains the trading logic for identifying pricing gaps and executing trades.
'''
from poloniex_api import PoloniexAPI
from coinex_api import CoinExAPI
from analytics import Analytics
class TradingBot:
    def __init__(self, config):
        self.config = config
        self.poloniex_api = PoloniexAPI()
        self.coinex_api = CoinExAPI()
        self.analytics = Analytics()
        self.position_size = self.config.get_setting('position_size')
    def identify_gaps(self, symbol):
        poloniex_order_book = self.poloniex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        coinex_order_book = self.coinex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        # Extract bid and ask prices
        poloniex_bid = float(poloniex_order_book['bids'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book['bids'] else 0
        poloniex_ask = float(poloniex_order_book['asks'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book['asks'] else 0
        coinex_bid = float(coinex_order_book['data']['bids'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book['data']['bids'] else 0
        coinex_ask = float(coinex_order_book['data']['asks'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book['data']['asks'] else 0
        # Identify pricing gaps
        if poloniex_bid > coinex_ask:
            return 'buy', coinex_ask, self.position_size
        elif coinex_bid > poloniex_ask:
            return 'sell', poloniex_ask, self.position_size
        return None, None, None
    def execute_trade(self, symbol, amount, direction):
        # Logic to execute trade
        if direction == 'buy':
            print(f"Buying {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            self.poloniex_api.place_order(symbol, amount, 'buy')
        elif direction == 'sell':
            print(f"Selling {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            self.coinex_api.place_order(symbol, amount, 'sell')
    def run(self, symbol):
        direction, price, amount = self.identify_gaps(symbol)
        if direction:
            self.execute_trade(symbol, amount, direction)
```

analytics.py
```python
'''
Contains the analytics logic for recalculating spreads and fees.
'''
class Analytics:
    def __init__(self):
        pass
    def calculate_spread(self, bid_price, ask_price):
        '''
        Calculates the spread between bid and ask prices.
        '''
        return ask_price - bid_price
    def calculate_fees(self, amount, fee_rate):
        '''
        Calculates the fees based on the amount and fee rate.
        '''
        return amount * fee_rate
    def recalculate_spreads_and_fees(self, bid_price, ask_price, fee_rate):
        '''
        Recalculates spreads and fees for given bid and ask prices.
        '''
        spread = self.calculate_spread(bid_price, ask_price)
        fees = self.calculate_fees(spread, fee_rate)
        return spread, fees
    def get_fee_rate(self, exchange):
        '''
        Retrieves the fee rate for the specified exchange.
        '''
        # Placeholder for actual fee rate retrieval logic
        if exchange == 'Poloniex':
            return 0.0025  # Example fee rate for Poloniex
        elif exchange == 'CoinEx':
            return 0.001  # Example fee rate for CoinEx
        return 0.0  # Default fee rate if not found
```

trading_bot.py
```python
'''
Contains the trading logic for identifying pricing gaps and executing trades.
'''
from poloniex_api import PoloniexAPI
from coinex_api import CoinExAPI
from analytics import Analytics

class TradingBot:
    def __init__(self, config):
        self.config = config
        self.poloniex_api = PoloniexAPI()
        self.coinex_api = CoinExAPI()
        self.analytics = Analytics()
        self.position_size = self.config.get_setting('position_size')

    def identify_gaps(self, symbol):
        poloniex_order_book = self.poloniex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        coinex_order_book = self.coinex_api.get_order_book(symbol)

        # Extract bid and ask prices
        poloniex_bid = float(poloniex_order_book['bids'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book.get('bids') else 0
        poloniex_ask = float(poloniex_order_book['asks'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book.get('asks') else 0
        coinex_bid = float(coinex_order_book['data']['bids'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book.get('data', {}).get('bids') else 0
        coinex_ask = float(coinex_order_book['data']['asks'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book.get('data', {}).get('asks') else 0

        # Identify pricing gaps
        if poloniex_bid > coinex_ask:
            return 'buy', coinex_ask, self.position_size
        elif coinex_bid > poloniex_ask:
            return 'sell', poloniex_ask, self.position_size
        return None, None, None

    def execute_trade(self, symbol, amount, direction):
        # Logic to execute trade
        if direction == 'buy':
            print(f"Buying {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            self.poloniex_api.place_order(symbol, amount, 'buy')
        elif direction == 'sell':
            print(f"Selling {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            self.coinex_api.place_order(symbol, amount, 'sell')

    def run(self, symbol):
        '''
        Runs the trading bot to identify gaps and execute trades.
        '''
        direction, price, amount = self.identify_gaps(symbol)
        if direction:
            self.execute_trade(symbol, amount, direction)
```

```python
'''
Main entry point for the cross-exchange trading bot.
'''
from config_manager import ConfigManager
from trading_bot import TradingBot
from gui import GUI

def main():
    config = ConfigManager('config.json')
    trading_bot = TradingBot(config)
    gui = GUI(trading_bot)
    gui.run()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

config_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles loading and managing configuration settings from a JSON file.
'''
import json

class ConfigManager:
    def __init__(self, config_file):
        self.config_file = config_file
        self.settings = self.load_config()

    def load_config(self):
        with open(self.config_file, 'r') as file:
            return json.load(file)

    def get_setting(self, key):
        return self.settings.get(key)
```

exchange_api.py
```python
'''
Abstract class for handling API interactions with exchanges.
'''
class ExchangeAPI:
    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        raise NotImplementedError

    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        raise NotImplementedError

    def place_order(self, symbol, amount, direction):
        raise NotImplementedError
```

poloniex_api.py
```python
'''
Implementation for Poloniex API.
'''
import requests
from exchange_api import ExchangeAPI

class PoloniexAPI(ExchangeAPI):
    BASE_URL = 'https://api.poloniex.com'

    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        try:
            response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/public?command=returnOrderBook&currencyPair={symbol}')
            response.raise_for_status()  # Raises an error for bad responses
            return response.json()
        except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
            print(f"Error fetching order book: {e}")
            return {}

    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        try:
            response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/public?command=returnFundingInfo&currency={symbol}')
            response.raise_for_status()
            return response.json()
        except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
            print(f"Error fetching funding rate: {e}")
            return {}

    def place_order(self, symbol, amount, direction):
        # Implement actual order placement logic here
        print(f"Placing {direction} order for {amount} of {symbol} on Poloniex.")
        # Example: Send a POST request to place the order (authentication required)
```

coinex_api.py
```python
'''
Implementation for CoinEx API.
'''
import requests
from exchange_api import ExchangeAPI

class CoinExAPI(ExchangeAPI):
    BASE_URL = 'https://api.coinex.com/v1'

    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        try:
            response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/market/depth?market={symbol}')
            response.raise_for_status()
            return response.json()
        except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
            print(f"Error fetching order book: {e}")
            return {}

    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        try:
            response = requests.get(f'{self.BASE_URL}/market/funding_rate?market={symbol}')
            response.raise_for_status()
            return response.json()
        except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
            print(f"Error fetching funding rate: {e}")
            return {}

    def place_order(self, symbol, amount, direction):
        # Implement actual order placement logic here
        print(f"Placing {direction} order for {amount} of {symbol} on CoinEx.")
        # Example: Send a POST request to place the order (authentication required)
```

trading_bot.py
```python
'''
Contains the trading logic for identifying pricing gaps and executing trades.
'''
from poloniex_api import PoloniexAPI
from coinex_api import CoinExAPI
from analytics import Analytics

class TradingBot:
    def __init__(self, config):
        self.config = config
        self.poloniex_api = PoloniexAPI()
        self.coinex_api = CoinExAPI()
        self.analytics = Analytics()
        self.position_size = self.config.get_setting('position_size')

    def identify_gaps(self, symbol):
        poloniex_order_book = self.poloniex_api.get_order_book(symbol)
        coinex_order_book = self.coinex_api.get_order_book(symbol)

        # Extract bid and ask prices
        poloniex_bid = float(poloniex_order_book['bids'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book.get('bids') else 0
        poloniex_ask = float(poloniex_order_book['asks'][0][0]) if poloniex_order_book.get('asks') else 0
        coinex_bid = float(coinex_order_book['data']['bids'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book.get('data', {}).get('bids') else 0
        coinex_ask = float(coinex_order_book['data']['asks'][0][0]) if coinex_order_book.get('data', {}).get('asks') else 0

        # Identify pricing gaps
        if poloniex_bid > coinex_ask:
            return 'buy', coinex_ask, self.position_size
        elif coinex_bid > poloniex_ask:
            return 'sell', poloniex_ask, self.position_size
        return None, None, None

    def execute_trade(self, symbol, amount, direction):
        # Logic to execute trade
        if direction == 'buy':
            print(f"Buying {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            self.poloniex_api.place_order(symbol, amount, 'buy')
        elif direction == 'sell':
            print(f"Selling {amount} of {symbol} at price.")
            self.coinex_api.place_order(symbol, amount, 'sell')

    def run(self, symbol):
        '''
        Runs the trading bot to identify gaps and execute trades.
        '''
        direction, price, amount = self.identify_gaps(symbol)
        if direction:
            self.execute_trade(symbol, amount, direction)
```

        '''
        Calculates the spread between bid and ask prices.
        '''
        return ask_price - bid_price

config_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles loading and managing configuration settings from a JSON file.
'''
import json
class ConfigManager:
    def __init__(self, config_file):
        self.config_file = config_file
        self.settings = self.load_config()
    def load_config(self):
        with open(self.config_file, 'r') as file:
            return json.load(file)
    def get_setting(self, key):
        return self.settings.get(key)
```

'''
Abstract class for handling API interactions with exchanges.
'''
class ExchangeAPI:
    def get_order_book(self, symbol):
        raise NotImplementedError
    def get_funding_rate(self, symbol):
        raise NotImplementedError
    def place_order(self, symbol, amount, direction):
        raise NotImplementedError
